	private static int lapg_next( int state, int symbol ) {
		int p;
		if( lapg_action[state] < -2 ) {
			for( p = - lapg_action[state] - 3; lapg_lalr[p] >= 0; p += 2 )
				if( lapg_lalr[p] == symbol ) break;
			return lapg_lalr[p+1];
		}
		return lapg_action[state];
	}

	private static int lapg_state_sym( int state, int symbol ) {
		int min = lapg_sym_goto[symbol], max = lapg_sym_goto[symbol+1]-1;
		int i, e;

		while( min <= max ) {
			e = (min + max) >> 1;
			i = lapg_sym_from[e];
			if( i == state )
				return lapg_sym_to[e];
			else if( i < state )
				min = e + 1;
			else
				max = e - 1;
		}
		return -1;
	}

	public boolean parse() {

		byte[]        token = new byte[4096];
		int           lapg_head = 0, group = 0, lapg_i, lapg_size, chr;
		lapg_symbol[] lapg_m = new lapg_symbol[1024];
		lapg_symbol   lapg_n;
		int           lapg_current_line = 1, lapg_current_offset = 0;
		int           lapg_symbols_ok = 4;

		lapg_m[0] = new lapg_symbol();
		lapg_m[0].state = 0;
		chr = buff[l++];if( l == end ) fillb();

		NEXTTOKEN:
		do {
			lapg_n = new lapg_symbol();
			lapg_n.pos = new lapg_place( lapg_current_line, lapg_current_offset );
			for( lapg_size = 0, lapg_i = group; lapg_i >= 0; ) {
				if( lapg_size < 4095 ) token[lapg_size++] = (byte)chr;
				lapg_i = lapg_lexem[lapg_i][lapg_char2no[(chr+256)%256]];
				if( lapg_i >= -1 && chr != 0 ) { 
					lapg_current_offset++;
					if( chr == '\n' ) lapg_current_line++;
					chr = buff[l++];if( l == end ) fillb();
				}
			}
			lapg_n.endpos = new lapg_place( lapg_current_line, lapg_current_offset );

			if( lapg_i == -1 ) {
				if( chr == 0 ) {
					error( "Unexpected end of file reached");
					break;
				}
				error( MessageFormat.format( "invalid lexem at line {0}: `{1}`, skipped", lapg_n.pos.line, new String(token,0,lapg_size) ) );
				lapg_n.lexem = -1;
				continue;
			}

			lapg_size--;
			lapg_n.lexem = -lapg_i-2;
			lapg_n.sym = null;

			switch( lapg_n.lexem ) {
				case 130:
					 continue; 
				case 131:
					 continue; 
				case 132:
					 group = @1;continue; 
				case 133:
					 continue; 
				case 134:
					 group = @0;continue; 
			}

			SKIPNEXTTOKEN: for(;;) {

			do {
				lapg_i = lapg_next( lapg_m[lapg_head].state, lapg_n.lexem );

				if( lapg_i >= 0 ) {
					lapg_symbol lapg_gg = new lapg_symbol();
					lapg_gg.sym = (lapg_rlen[lapg_i]!=0)?lapg_m[lapg_head+1-lapg_rlen[lapg_i]].sym:null;
					lapg_gg.lexem = lapg_rlex[lapg_i];
					lapg_gg.state = 0;
					if( DEBUG_SYNTAX )
						System.out.println( "reduce to " + lapg_syms[lapg_rlex[lapg_i]] );
					lapg_gg.pos = (lapg_rlen[lapg_i]!=0)?lapg_m[lapg_head+1-lapg_rlen[lapg_i]].pos:lapg_n.pos;
					lapg_gg.endpos = (lapg_rlen[lapg_i]!=0)?lapg_m[lapg_head].endpos:lapg_n.pos;
					switch( lapg_i ) {
						case 24:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 25:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 26:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 27:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 28:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 29:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 30:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 33:
							 $$ = new Node( Kind.Identifier, null, null, null ); break; 
							break;
						case 76:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 77:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 78:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 79:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 80:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 81:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 82:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 83:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 84:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 85:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 86:
							 $$ = new Node( Kind.Dot, $primary_expression, null, null ); break; 
							break;
						case 87:
							 $$ = new Node( Kind.TypeDot, null, null, null ); break; 
							break;
						case 90:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 91:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 92:
							 $$ = new Node( Kind.DimmedExpr, null, null, $primary_expression_na ); break; 
							break;
						case 93:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 98:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 99:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 100:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 102:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 103:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 104:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 105:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 106:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 107:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 109:
							 $$ = $1;
		// HACK to resolve Cast ambiguity
		if( CastExpr($expression,lapg_n) ) {
			// perform reduce
			for( int e = lapg_rlen[lapg_i]; e > 0; e-- ) lapg_m[lapg_head--].sym = null;
			lapg_m[++lapg_head] = lapg_gg;
			lapg_m[lapg_head].state = lapg_state_sym( lapg_m[lapg_head-1].state, lapg_gg.lexem );
			if( lapg_m[lapg_head].state != -1 ) {
				// shift cast_token (if possible)
				lapg_gg.lexem = (int)Tokens.cast_token;
				lapg_gg.sym = null;
				lapg_gg.state = lapg_state_sym( lapg_m[lapg_head].state, lapg_gg.lexem );
				lapg_gg.pos = lapg_gg.endpos = lapg_n.pos;
				if( lapg_gg.state != -1 )
					lapg_m[++lapg_head] = lapg_gg;
			}
			// skip default reduce code
			continue;
		}
		break; 
							break;
						case 110:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 111:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 113:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 114:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 115:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 117:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 118:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 120:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 121:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 123:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 124:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 125:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 126:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 127:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 128:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 130:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 131:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 133:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 135:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 137:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 139:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 141:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 143:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
						case 144:
							 $$ = new Node(); break; 
							break;
					}
					for( int e = lapg_rlen[lapg_i]; e > 0; e-- ) 
						lapg_m[lapg_head--] = null;
					lapg_m[++lapg_head] = lapg_gg;
					lapg_m[lapg_head].state = lapg_state_sym( lapg_m[lapg_head-1].state, lapg_gg.lexem );
				} else if( lapg_i == -1 ) {
					lapg_m[++lapg_head] = lapg_n;
					lapg_m[lapg_head].state = lapg_state_sym( lapg_m[lapg_head-1].state, lapg_n.lexem );
					lapg_symbols_ok++;
					if( DEBUG_SYNTAX )
						System.out.println( MessageFormat.format( "shift: {0} ({1})", lapg_syms[lapg_n.lexem], new String(token,0,lapg_size) ) );
				}

			} while( lapg_i >= 0 && lapg_m[lapg_head].state != -1 );

			if( (lapg_i == -2 || lapg_m[lapg_head].state == -1) && lapg_n.lexem != 0 ) {
				while( lapg_head >= 0 && lapg_state_sym( lapg_m[lapg_head].state, 2 ) == -1 ) {
					lapg_m[lapg_head] = null;
					lapg_head--;
				}
				if( lapg_head >= 0 ) {
					lapg_m[++lapg_head] = new lapg_symbol();
					lapg_m[lapg_head].lexem = 2;
					lapg_m[lapg_head].sym = null;
					lapg_m[lapg_head].state = lapg_state_sym( lapg_m[lapg_head-1].state, 2 );
					lapg_m[lapg_head].pos = lapg_n.pos;
					if( lapg_symbols_ok >= 4 )
						error( MessageFormat.format( "syntax error before line {0}", lapg_n.pos.line ) );

					lapg_i = lapg_symbols_ok;
					lapg_symbols_ok = 0;
					if( lapg_i > 1 )
						continue SKIPNEXTTOKEN;
					else
						continue NEXTTOKEN;
				} else {
					lapg_head = 0;
					lapg_m[0] = new lapg_symbol();
					lapg_m[0].state = 0;
				}
				break;
			}
			break;
			}

		} while( lapg_n.lexem != 0 );

		if( lapg_m[lapg_head].state != 730 && lapg_symbols_ok >= 4 ) {
			error( MessageFormat.format( "syntax error before line {0}", lapg_n.pos.line ) );
			return false;
		};
		return true;
	}
}
